#3 types de bank privé
# global_arbitrage_bank
# national_financial_investor
# domestic_bank

total_bank_funds = {
	value = private_bank_funds
	add = funds_from_foreign_debt_total
	add = private_bank_foreign_reserves_per_bank 
 	add = private_bank_gold_reserve_bank
	add = private_bank_silver_reserve_bank_in_gold  
} 
private_bank_funds_per_private_bank = {
	value = private_bank_funds
	divide = total_privat_bank
}
total_privat_bank = {
	every_in_list = {
		variable = privat_bank_variable_list_ordered
		add  = 1
	}
} 
private_bank_funds_per_private_bank_add_foreign_debt = { #valeur que détient une bank dans la ligne GUI -> pour gui +++ besoins de scope
	value = owner.private_bank_funds_per_private_bank
	add = funds_from_foreign_debt
	add = private_bank_foreign_reserves_per_bank_gui 
	add = private_bank_gold_reserve_per_bank_gui
	add = private_bank_silver_reserve_per_bank_gui_in_gold 
}

private_bank_silver_reserve_per_bank_gui_in_gold = {
	value = private_bank_silver_reserve_per_bank_gui
	multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
}
private_bank_gold_reserve_per_bank_gui = {
	value = 0
	############################
	#company_Rothschild_Bank_gbr gold
	############################ 
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_company_type = company_type:company_Rothschild_Bank_gbr
		}
		add = company_Rothschild_Bank_gbr_gold_stockpile
	}
	############################
	#company_Rothschild_Bank_fra gold
	############################ 
	if = {
		limit = {
